Welcome to Arstotzka!
You have been chosen to be an Inspector on the gate to Arstotzka. Check papers and if everything seems to be Ok let them through (send 'Accept') and if there is anything wrong don't let them go to Arstotzka!! (send 'Reject'). Remember to allow only adults. (from 18 years old)
To get the list of countries that shouldn't be with listed cities under them type 'i'
If you are ready to play just type 's' : 
s
